Government Notification
Sri Lanka Export Development Act, No. 40 of 1979
Order under Section 14

By virtue of the powers vested in me by Section 14 of the Sri Lanka Export Development Act,
No. 40 of 1979, I, Ranil Wickremesinghe, Minister of Investment Promotion with the
concurrence of the Minister of Finance, Economic Stabilization and National Policies, do by
this Order amend the rate of CESS specified in the corresponding entry in Column IV in the
Schedule to the Extraordinary Gazette No. 2202/6 dated 17.11.2020, in respect of the articles
described under the H.S. Codes as specified in the Schedule hereto, with effect from Novenber

os 2. sl

Ranil Weems |
Minister of Investment Promotion

Government Notification
Sri Lanka Export Development Act, No. 40 of 1979
Order under Section 14

By virtue of the powers vested in me by Section 14 of the Sri Lanka Export Development Act,
No. 40 of 1979, I, Ranil Wickremesinghe, Minister of Investment Promotion with the
concurrence of the Minister of Finance, Economic Stabilization and National Policies, do by
this Order amend the rate of CESS specified in the corresponding entry in Column IV in the
Schedule to the Extraordinary Gazette No. 2202/6 dated 17.11.2020, in respect of the articles
described under the H.S. Codes as specified in the Schedule hereto, with effect from Novenber

os 2. sl

Ranil Weems |

Government Notification
Sri Lanka Export Development Act, No. 40 of 1979
Order under Section 14

By virtue of the powers vested in me by Section 14 of the Sri Lanka Export Development Act,
No. 40 of 1979, I, Ranil Wickremesinghe, Minister of Investment Promotion with the
concurrence of the Minister of Finance, Economic Stabilization and National Policies, do by
this Order amend the rate of CESS specified in the corresponding entry in Column IV in the
Schedule to the Extraordinary Gazette No. 2202/6 dated 17.11.2020, in respect of the articles
described under the H.S. Codes as specified in the Schedule hereto, with effect from Novenber

Ay 2022.

a \ |

MEA pb Abete! y
Ranil Wickremesinghe |
Minister of Investment Prémotion

Government Notification
Sri Lanka Export Development Act, No. 40 of 1979
Order under Section 14

By virtue of the powers vested in me by Section 14 of the Sri Lanka Export Development Act,
No. 40 of 1979, I, Ranil Wickremesinghe, Minister of Investment Promotion with the
concurrence of the Minister of Finance, Economic Stabilization and National Policies, do by
this Order amend the rate of CESS specified in the corresponding entry in Column IV in the
Schedule to the Extraordinary Gazette No. 2202/6 dated 17.11.2020, in respect of the articles
described under the H.S. Codes as specified in the Schedule hereto, with effect from Novenber

Ay 2022.

a \ |

MEA pb Abete! y
Ranil Wickremesinghe |
Minister of Investment Prémotion

November .. \S..., 2022
Ministry of Investment Promotion
